\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00857}00857 \textcolor{comment}{  /// The nodal coordinates are used in the elements' mapping}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00858}00858 \textcolor{comment}{  /// between local and global coordinates and in the simplest}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00859}00859 \textcolor{comment}{  /// case (stationary nodes in Lagrange-\/type elements) this mapping}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00860}00860 \textcolor{comment}{  /// is given by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00861}00861 \textcolor{comment}{  /// \(\backslash\)f[  x\_i = \(\backslash\)sum\_\{j=1\}\string^\{N\_\{node\}\} X\_\{ij\} \(\backslash\)psi\_\{j\}(s\_k) \(\backslash\)f]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00862}00862 \textcolor{comment}{  /// so we need only access to the nodal coordinates}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00863}00863 \textcolor{comment}{  /// \(\backslash\)f\$ X\_\{ij\}\(\backslash\) (i=1..DIM) \(\backslash\)f\$ of all nodes \(\backslash\)f\$ j \(\backslash\)f\$ : provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00864}00864 \textcolor{comment}{  /// by the Node member function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00865}00865 \textcolor{comment}{  /// \(\backslash\)code Node::x(i) \(\backslash\)endcode}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00866}00866 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00867}00867 \textcolor{comment}{  /// If the nodal positions are time-\/dependent, the mapping becomes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00868}00868 \textcolor{comment}{  /// \(\backslash\)f[  x\_i(t) = \(\backslash\)sum\_\{j=1\}\string^\{N\_\{node\}\}  X\_\{ij\}(t) \(\backslash\) \(\backslash\)psi\_\{j\}(s\_k). \(\backslash\)f]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00869}00869 \textcolor{comment}{  /// Within the computation (where time is only evaluated at discrete}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00870}00870 \textcolor{comment}{  /// levels) this becomes}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00872}00872 \textcolor{comment}{  /// and we need access to the nodal coordinates \(\backslash\)f\$ X\_\{ijt\} \(\backslash\) (i=1..DIM) \(\backslash\)f\$}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00873}00873 \textcolor{comment}{  /// of all nodes \(\backslash\)f\$ j \(\backslash\)f\$ at the present (t=0) and previous (t>0) timesteps:}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00876}00876 \textcolor{comment}{  /// \(\backslash\)b Note: The interpretation of the history values is slightly more}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00883}00883 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00884}00884 \textcolor{comment}{  /// Finally, some elements employ mappings}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00885}00885 \textcolor{comment}{  /// that involve additional, generalised coordinates. For instance,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00886}00886 \textcolor{comment}{  /// in Hermite elements the mapping between local and global coordinates}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00887}00887 \textcolor{comment}{  /// is based on an independent interpolation for the global coordinates}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00889}00889 \textcolor{comment}{  /// elements, the mapping becomes}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00891}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceoomph_aff0c55ce31f12df52b2fe5ae647ffebe}{00891}} \textcolor{comment}{  ///    \(\backslash\)psi\_\{jk\}(s\_k) \(\backslash\)f]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00892}00892 \textcolor{comment}{  /// where \(\backslash\)f\$ N\_\{type\} \(\backslash\)f\$ is the number of the different types of generalised}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00894}00894 \textcolor{comment}{  /// \(\backslash\)f\$ N\_\{type\}=2 \(\backslash\)f\$ and k=0 corresponds to the global coordinates while}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l00897}00897 \textcolor{comment}{  /// In such cases we need access to the generalised nodal coordinates}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l01673}01673   \textcolor{comment}{//=====================================================================}\textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l01674}01674 \textcolor{comment}{  /// A Class for nodes that deform elastically (i.e. position is an}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l01675}01675 \textcolor{comment}{  /// unknown in the problem). The idea is that the Eulerian positions are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l01676}01676 \textcolor{comment}{  /// stored in a Data object and the Lagrangian coordinates are stored in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l01677}01677 \textcolor{comment}{  /// addition. The pointer that addresses the Eulerian positions is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l01678}01678 \textcolor{comment}{  /// set to the pointer to Value in the Data object. Hence,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l01679}01679 \textcolor{comment}{  /// SolidNode uses knowledge of the internal structure of Data and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l01680}01680 \textcolor{comment}{  /// must be a friend of the Data class.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l01681}01681 \textcolor{comment}{  /// In order to allow a mesh to deform via an elastic-\/style}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l01682}01682 \textcolor{comment}{  /// equation in deforming-\/domain problems,  the positions are stored}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l01683}01683 \textcolor{comment}{  /// separately from the values, so that elastic problems may be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l01684}01684 \textcolor{comment}{  /// combined with any other type of problem.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nodes_8h_source_l01685}01685 \textcolor{comment}{}  \textcolor{comment}{//=====================================================================}}
